Typically hard money lenders will lend 50-70% of the value of the property regardless of the sales price (unlike banks). This is a public document that is recorded.\r\n* Tax liens - Each state creates the system and rules for the lien or deed process so careful research is necessary. When you turn on the timer and keep focused till the end of the pomodoro - you get rewarded with a nice red Pomodoro. \r\n\r\nIn other cases, when you get distracted or stop focusing early - you get a green Pomodoro.\r\n\r\nOverall it features: \r\n- tracking a focused activity separately from distracted;\r\n- tracking individual contexts that important for you;\r\n- weekly and monthly statistics for analysis;  \r\n\r\nAll that can help you to develop the following habits to fight procrastination. \r\n- be focused in a context from the beginning to the end of the Pomodoro. Instead of focusing on just turning it on;\r\n- to work on efficiency by striving to increase the number of red tomatoes with respect to green ones;\r\n- be aware of the actual distribution of your time within the important contexts of yours;\r\n\r\n\"The Pomodoro Technique\"® and \"Pomodoro\"® are registered trademarks by Francesco Cirillo. Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a “handwritten” font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. The capabilities of MuseScore can be extended via plugins, and the growing repository on musescore.org contains many plugins submitted by users.\r\n\r\nMuseScore includes a set of sounds that reproduce common instruments (as defined by General MIDI) without taking up a lot of disk space or memory, but you can also substitute any SoundFont you prefer for a wider variety of sounds or for more realism.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can import and export MIDI and MusicXML files, and it can also import from Capella and several other programs.
